)@@G@@    END       MAIN___   *[S@@@*SDFF*@[@@@AC     @C@@@AC  THIS PROGRAM WRBL
)@@G@@ITES OUT PAR DIRECTIVES THAT  @B@@@AC  ARE USED IN THE ANALISYS OF IO DABM
)@@G@@TA.   @]@@@AC  INPUT IS:@B@@@AC  1. NUMBER OF DEVICES (KNOWN TO PAR)    BN
)@@G@@@A@@@AC  2.  RAW IO CONFIG DATA FROM PAR  @[@@@AC     @^@@@AC  TERRY MULBO
)@@G@@LINS - BCSR @[@@@AC     @ @@@]      DIMENSION TABLE(10000)  @A@@@#      BP
)@@G@@DIMENSION IVAL(200),LDAT(200) @^@@@#      DATA KOUNT/0/     @#@@@]      BQ
)@@G@@READ*,LEN   @A@@@]      READ(5,5) ( TABLE(I),I=1,LEN) @^@@@]5     FORMATBR
)@@G@@(6(O12,1X)) @^@@@]      DO 100 M=1,LEN,4  @A@#@]      LDAT=BITS(TABLE(M+BS
)@@G@@1),1,12)-1  @A@@@#      L=BITS(TABLE(M+1),1,12)-1     @A@@@]      INDEX=BT
)@@G@@BITS(TABLE(M+2),1,12)   @#@#@]      IVAL=999    @]@@@#      IV=999@ @#@]BU
)@@G@@      IF(INDEX.EQ.1 ) IVAL=0  @ @@@#      IF(INDEX.EQ.1 ) IV=0    @ @#@]BV
)@@G@@      IF(INDEX.EQ.3 ) IVAL=1  @ @@@#      IF(INDEX.EQ.3 ) IV=1    @ @#@]BW
)@@G@@      IF(INDEX.EQ.5 ) IVAL=2  @ @@@#      IF(INDEX.EQ.5 ) IV=2    @ @#@]BX
)@@G@@      IF(INDEX.EQ.7 ) IVAL=3  @ @@@#      IF(INDEX.EQ.7 ) IV=3    @ @#@]BY
)@@G@@      IF(INDEX.EQ.9 ) IVAL=4  @ @@@#      IF(INDEX.EQ.9 ) IV=4    @ @#@]BZ
)@@G@@      IF(INDEX.EQ.11) IVAL=5  @ @@@#      IF(INDEX.EQ.11) IV=5    @A@#@]CA
)@@G@@      IF(IVAL.EQ.999) GO TO 100     @ @@@#      IF(IV.EQ.999) GO TO 100 CB
)@@G@@@^@@@]      KOUNT=KOUNT+1     @E@#@]      WRITE(7,7) IVAL,IVAL,LDAT,LDATCC
)@@G@@,IVAL,IVAL,LDAT,LDAT,   @^@@@#      IVAL(KOUNT)=IV    @D@#@]     $  IVALCD
)@@G@@,IVAL,LDAT,IVAL,IVAL,LDAT,IVAL,IVAL,LDAT, @^@@@#      LDAT(KOUNT)=L     CE
)@@G@@@D@#@]     $  IVAL,IVAL,LDAT,LDAT,IVAL,IVAL,LDAT,IVAL,IVAL  @[@#@]C     CF
)@@G@@@F@#@]7     FORMAT('TTLREQS(',I1,'):=TTLREQS(',I1,')+SBUREQ[0,',I2,']+',CG
)@@G@@@A@#@]     $       'SBUREQ[1,',I2,']'/    @E@#@]     $  'TTLWDS(',I1,'):CH
)@@G@@=TTLWDS(',I1,')+SBUREQ[2,',I2,']+', @A@#@]     $       'SBUREQ[3,',I2,']CI
)@@G@@'/    @E@#@]     $  'SVCTIM(',I1,'):=SVCTIM(',I1,')+SBUREQ[4,',I2,']'/  CJ
)@@G@@@E@#@]     $  'UNITACT(',I1,'):=UNITACT(',I1,')+SBUREQ[5,',I2,']'/@E@#@]CK
)@@G@@     $  'REQSQD(',I1,'):=REQSQD(',I1,')+SBUREQ[6,',I2,']'/  @E@#@]     $CL
)@@G@@  'CUMQSIZ(',I1,'):=CUMQSIZ(',I1,')+SBUREQ[7,',I2,']'/@A@#@]     $  'IF CM
)@@G@@SBUREQ[4,',I2,'] <> 0 '/@D@#@]     $  'TALLYBUSY(',I1,'):=TALLYBUSY(',I1CN
)@@G@@,')+1'/     @E@#@]     $  'DEVPROB:=(1000*SBUREQ[4,',I2,']+ROUND)/DELTATCO
)@@G@@ '/   @D@#@]     $  'TTLPROB:=((1000-DEVPROB)*TTLPROB)/1000 '/    @G@#@]CP
)@@G@@     $  'BUSYPROB(',I1,'):=((1000-DEVPROB)*BUSYPROB(',I1,'))/1000 '/    CQ
)@@G@@@#@#@]     $  'ENDIF')  @D@#@]      WRITE(6,6)  (TABLE(MMM),MMM=M,M+3),ICR
)@@G@@VAL,LDAT    @C@#@]6     FORMAT(1X,4O13,'  IVAL=',I5,'   LDAT=',I5)@#@@@]CS
